< text>
I first visited Dr. Panahpour in Feb. 2018 due to a chronic discomfort in a molar that had been filled by my previous dentist 10 years earlier. About five years ago, a small blister showed up on the outside gum line adjacent to the tooth but my dentist could not find nothing wrong. It was also about this time I began having symptoms of heart arrhythmia and heart flutter that would at first last for a few seconds, but over time increased in frequency and severity for up to several hours. These attacks had gotten to the point I was seriously considering seeking the care of a cardiologist. Through the use of CT scan and digital x-ray, Dr. Panahpour found a large infection (cavitation) in the jaw involving the roots of the tooth and also diagnosed that the tooth itself was dead. After three months of preparation, the tooth was extracted. The tooth was so far gone it broke into little pieces as it was removed, but all the infection and rotted bone was finally removed including calcified cysts in the jaw that had bonded to the roots. My bodies relief from the removal of the infection after all those years of harboring it was immediate. I also had no pain during the entire procedure, even after the anesthetic wore off, and had minimal swelling and bleeding afterwards. Dr. Panahpour has since removed infected/rotted bone in two 20 year-old wisdom tooth sites and one 30 year old site as well the past year with the infection verified by pathogen reports from an independent lab. The unexpected benefits from the infection being cleaned out, however, was that my heart arrhythmia and heart flutter attacks all but disappeared immediately, chronic sinus drainage quit, tinnitus in my left ear eased considerably, inflammation in my larynx disappeared with full range of my singing voice returning, and my close-up vision improved to the point I only need to use my reading glasses for small print. Last winter and spring Dr. Panahpour also began treating my TMJ. Again, I was totally caught off guard by the health benefits that happened over the next several months as he made adjustments on my dental appliance to correct this condition: 1) Regular dream-sleep occurs almost nightly (it had been years since I'd had regular dream sleep); 2) my posture became more balanced and a chronic ache in my left hip all but disappeared; 3) all my teeth contact evenly now and my chewing action is balanced between the left and right sides. My wife has also had six cavitations cleaned out by Dr. Panahpour (four old wisdom tooth sites and two root canal sites) with many health benefits ranging from 30+ pounds of weight loss to clearer sinuses, far greater energy, and a much greater resistance to colds and flu. I noticed Quackwatch downplays these treatments as "unproven" procedures. They may be "unproven" but they have changed me and my wife's life. We would eagerly do all the treatments again if needed. We've gained our health back and feel better than when we were in our 40's (we are 60 this year). Quackwatch also mentions Dr. Panahpour's poor GPA. It wouldn't surprise me at all if his GPA was low as pioneers who think and practice "outside the box" always pay the consequences when attempting to work in the traditional main-stream system. Finally, I found it odd that my original review had been removed from Google several month ago as had the reviews of many of Dr. Panahpours patients who had also shared specific health benefits from his treatments; however, when I checked the reviews again a few days ago, my original posting had been put back and this updated one removed, so I‚Äôm reposting this updated one as it contains additional health benefits since my most recent cavitation surgery in his office in California. Notwithstanding, God has blessed Dr. Panahpour with insights and a passion for his trade and a compassion for his patients that is rare to find!< /text>

<text>I had my first appointment with Dr. Panahpour in December 2011, when I was severely ill with chronic Lyme disease. My severe illness impacted my nervous system to such a degree that I had nearly constant full body tremors, daily convulsions, and occasional paralysis.  I was housebound and occasionally bedbound; on my rare trips out of the house for doctor appointments aided by my husband, I was confined to a wheelchair.  It was in this state that I met Dr. Panahpour.

His high level of skill and experience was immediately apparent as he made recommendations for the surgeries and other suggestions to help the surgeries be more successful.  He took much more time to talk with me and my husband than would be typical for an appointment, and we had the sense that he really wanted to make sure we understood and were comfortable with every aspect of his care.  His knowledge wasn't bound by the typical conventional experience of most dentists, as he had advanced training, and that level of knowledge was very clear to both of us at a time when I needed a high level of consideration in my medical care.

In addition to this, I must share that the warmth and authentic kindness I felt from Dr. Panahpour immediately put me at ease.  Even when I struggled to speak due to nervous system issues, he was patient and present, and made me feel like a real person, rather than a disabled nobody. I love this vet. I've been going for 5 years and gone through end stage of life with my senior cats , and growing pains with my kittens. I spent 15 years at the horrible Gateway Animal Hospital until they killed my cat Wolfie. Literally pulled the fur off his neck dragging him out of the carrier. I tried Wayfarers, a small operation run by a single well meaning vet. I didn't feel they were up to speed, but  Nemo was accustomed to them so I continued until he passed from old age. People.  Do NOT TAKE YOUR BELOVED PET TO THIS HORRIBLE HOSPITAL.

I took my bird to have her checked out.  I was told there was no hope for her and she must be euthanized to end her suffering.  So I asked that I spend our last moments together with her as she is put to sleep.

<rate>5<//rate>< Text>
I have been taking my cats to Dr. Hussein at GSAH for about 8 years now and would recommend him as a skilled veterinarian without reservation.  His approach to veterinary medicine is somewhat conservative, which I appreciate.  He is cautious and thoughtful, never recommending expensive or invasive tests or treatment unless absolutely necessary.

He has an uncannily natural way with animals that I‚Äôve never encountered in a veterinarian before.  My cats are strangely calm in his presence, even if they‚Äôre getting a thermometer put up their butt!  And the few times they have started to squirm or panic, Dr. Hussein handled it with calm expertise.

I also have to rave about the GSAH staff (especially Adele!).  They are so friendly, accommodating and, like Dr. Hussein, really care about animals.  Even though they see many animals every day, they still always manage to make me feel that my cats are special and unique.  In general, I love going there since the office is such a comfortable, friendly place to bring my animals.

When my cat, Bello, of 13 years, was in his final months and days of life, after being treated by Dr. Hussein in many of his ‚Äúgolden years‚Äù, Dr. Hussein and the GSAH staff went above and beyond what I‚Äôd ever expect in their showing of support and sympathy.  This meant so much to me, since I knew they truly understood how much I cared about Bello and what a great loss it was to me.

Finally, I should mention that I‚Äôve never had to wait long to see a vet there or to make an appointment and the prices at GSAH are super reasonable.  Often, I‚Äôve gotten freebie samples of products as well‚Äîcat food or flea treatment, for example.  I highly recommend Dr. Hussein and GSAH in general.</Text>

< review>
I have been taking my cats to Dr. Hussein at GSAH for about 8 years now and would recommend him as a skilled veterinarian without reservation.  His approach to veterinary medicine is somewhat conservative, which I appreciate.  He is cautious and thoughtful, never recommending expensive or invasive tests or treatment unless absolutely necessary.

He has an uncannily natural way with animals that I‚Äôve never encountered in a veterinarian before.  My cats are strangely calm in his presence, even if they‚Äôre getting a thermometer put up their butt!  And the few times they have started to squirm or panic, Dr. Hussein handled it with calm expertise.

I also have to rave about the GSAH staff (especially Adele!).  They are so friendly, accommodating and, like Dr. Hussein, really care about animals.  Even though they see many animals every day, they still always manage to make me feel that my cats are special and unique.  In general, I love going there since the office is such a comfortable, friendly place to bring my animals.

When my cat, Bello, of 13 years, was in his final months and days of life, after being treated by Dr. Hussein in many of his ‚Äúgolden years‚Äù, Dr. Hussein and the GSAH staff went above and beyond what I‚Äôd ever expect in their showing of support and sympathy.  This meant so much to me, since I knew they truly understood how much I cared about Bello and what a great loss it was to me.

Finally, I should mention that I‚Äôve never had to wait long to see a vet there or to make an appointment and the prices at GSAH are super reasonable.  Often, I‚Äôve gotten freebie samples of products as well‚Äîcat food or flea treatment, for example.  I highly recommend Dr. Hussein and GSAH in general.</review>

< review>
Great healthy option whether you like meat or are a vegetarian.

For my fellow meat lovers the regular chicken bowl all veggie no rice is only $6.90 or $8.15 if you upgrade to white meat which I always do. It's under 500 calories which I like and I think closer to 400.

They also have beef bowls and tofu bowls for my vegetarian friends.

Overall a  good place to eat a healthy meal.<//review>

Excellent food, affordable prices, ample portions, good vibes, friendly, knowledgeable staff. 100% vegan. Tasty authentic Mexican, vegan organic in addition to being so good! Food is as good as what you'd get eating in someone's home who is really good cook. We had tamales, of course, and their goodness rivaled that of my favorite Texas tamale offerings. Enjoyed Flacos taquitos, black beans & rice at recent Vegan Soul Wellness Festival. And, yeah, they sold out before Festival ended, so missed out on banana leaf wrapped tamales, which Festival attendees raved about.</Text>

<text>I wanted to give this place 4.5 stars, because I really really like this place a lot. The food is really good, the prices are decent, and the service is nice. I am a person who has a lot of dietary restrictions, so when I get eat more than two things on the menu at a place, I need to check it out. When I went, it became my favorite place to go. There are a lot of options (it is all vegan, with a lot of GF stuff). The only reason it doesn't get all of the stars is because you have to wait a while to get the food. To be fair to them, the  kitchen space is small, and they are pretty busy a lot of the time. However, the extra time for food is worth it.</text>< pics>
